<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излить.html>изли́ть</a> (27275)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излить.html>изли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изливать.html>излива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour out, to vent (emotions, etc.)</li></ol>

***излишество.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излишество.html>изли́шество</a> (15376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изли́ш(ний)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlíš(nij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a> (17245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by chasing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полиция.html>поли́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повальный.html>пова́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обыск.html>о́быски</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продажный.html>прода́жных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Polícija proizvodíla poválʹnyje óbyski i <b>izlovíla</b> bóleje sótni prodážnyx žénščin</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Police conducted searches en masse and <b>caught</b> more than a hundred corrupt women</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́дите</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>изловлю́</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy uvídite, kak lóvko ja jevó <b>izlovljú</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You will see how shrewdly I will <b>catch</b> him/it!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a> (14315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">излучи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izlučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izlučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">излучи́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to radiate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:излучать.html>излуча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:уверенность.html>уве́ренность</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izlučátʹ</b> rádostʹ (uvérennostʹ)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to radiate happiness (confidence)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***измена.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a> (6240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izména</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>betrayal, treason
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>Ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gosudárstvennaja izména; izména Rodine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">high treason</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unfaithfulness, faithlessness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:супружеский.html>супру́жеская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">suprúžeskaja izména</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unfaithfulness, (conjugal) infidelity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
